< Text>
Visited El Mariachi's for a special occasion. They have done in and was a good choice for us. The food was good, served hot (careful, the plates are very hot). Wait time from order to food wasn't horrible, being as 12 others arrived before our family arrived. The restaurant was fairly busy. They do limit capacity and take precautions. We felt safe eating here.</Text>

<review>This is our go to Mexican restaurant and also our default take out option when we've had a busy day.

We sit down here once every couple months, but normally just order take-out or entree express. We've never had a bad meal here, the food is always good, and there is A LOT of it. Cheap too, we spend about an average of $30 - $40 for a family of four, including two 10 year old boys with hollow legs.

The atmosphere is welcoming and traditional, they always have drink specials, and they have a killer salsa bar. (Almost literally once... the green paste is NOT avocado, it's pureed jalapenos lol, yikes)

The boys always split a machos nachos, which is steak fries smothered  in nacho cheese and all the fixins. Not necessarily Mexican food, but they really like it. I recommend the rolled taquitos, and hubby always gets some sort of burrito smothered in some sort of sauce. (I'm extremely observant, I know) We always have leftovers for lunch the next day.

I highly recommend El Mariachis. It's good food and it's cheap. And there are so many ways to get it, whether going in, calling and picking it up, or having it delivered. (That's $8 extra tho)

SammiSue</review><Pics>None</Pics>< response>

Had not been in many years. Used to go a lot as a kid, and few times as a teenager, but went back with the family and was disappointed.

It wasn't bad, but the price-to-awesome ratio was skewed more towards the price side of things. We spent more, and didn't get to leave with leftovers!

Overall, not enough deliciousness to warrant the price. Could have ordered a variety of things elsewhere, left with leftovers, and still have spent the same or less. Food would have been awesome acrissed the board instead of "oh, this must been sitting awhile."
